
event `Senza Solaria Stocks Wardragon`
	shipyard "Senza Solaria Ships"
		`Wardragon`

mission `Senza Solaria Supply Wardragon`
	invisible
	landing
	source
		planet "Senza Solaria"
	to offer
		and	
			has `ship model: Wardragon`
			not `flagship model: Wardragon`
	on offer
		conversation
			scene "thumbnail/wardragon"
			`Upon arriving at Senza Solaria With your Wardragon, before you can even decide where to go, a group of researchers are already there to meet you the moment you step off of your ship.`
			`	"Our scanners detected a ship unknown to them within your fleet, would you be willing to donate it for us to research it?" says a researcher.`
			choice
				`	(Donate the Wardragon to be researched.) WARNING: ALL INSTALLED OUTFITS WILL BE LOST.`
					goto donate
				`	(Don't donate.)`
					defer
			label donate
			`"Ah, perfect! We appreciate your donation, and assure you, your contribution will not go to waste!"`
			`The engineers guide your ship to an isolated landing pad a few miles from the spaceport, and carefully transport it inside of one of their research facilities."`
			``
			`	After idling at the spaceport for a few hours, you hear rumors of a new ship entering production soon at Senza Solaria.`
				accept
	on accept
		take ship `Wardragon`
			"count" 1
		event `Senza Solaria Stocks Wardragon`

	to offer
		and	
			has `ship model: Polari`
			not `flagship model: Polari`
	on offer
		conversation
			scene "thumbnail/avgi polari"
			`Upon arriving at Senza Solaria With your Polari, before you can even decide where to go, a group of researchers are already there to meet you the moment you step off of your ship.`

			choice
				`	(Donate the Polari to be researched.) WARNING: ALL INSTALLED OUTFITS WILL BE LOST.`
					goto donate
				`	(Don't donate.)`
					defer
			label donate
			`"Ah, perfect! We appreciate your donation, and assure you, your contribution will not go to waste!"`
			`The engineers guide your ship to an isolated landing pad a few miles from the spaceport, and carefully transport it inside of one of their research facilities."`
			``
			`	After idling at the spaceport for a few hours, you hear rumors of a new ship entering production soon at Senza Solaria.`

		`Aberrant Junior`

mission `Senza Solaria Supply Aberrant Junior`
	invisible
	landing
	source
		planet "Senza Solaria"
	to offer
		and	
			has `ship model: Aberrant Junior`
			not `flagship model: Aberrant Junior`
	on offer
		conversation
			scene "thumbnail/aberrant junior"
			`Upon arriving at Senza Solaria With your Aberrant Junior, before you can even decide where to go, a group of researchers are already there to meet you the moment you step off of your ship.`
			`	"Our scanners detected a ship unknown to them within your fleet, would you be willing to donate it for us to research it?" says a researcher.`
			choice
				`	(Donate the Aberrant Junior to be researched.) WARNING: ALL INSTALLED OUTFITS WILL BE LOST.`
					goto donate
				`	(Don't donate.)`
					defer
			label donate
			`"Ah, perfect! We appreciate your donation, and assure you, your contribution will not go to waste!"`
			`The engineers guide your ship to an isolated landing pad a few miles from the spaceport, and carefully transport it inside of one of their research facilities."`
			``
			`	After idling at the spaceport for a few hours, you hear rumors of a new ship entering production soon at Senza Solaria.`
				accept
	on accept
		take ship `Aberrant Junior`
			"count" 1
		event `Senza Solaria Stocks Aberrant Junior`

	landing
	source
		planet "Senza Solaria"
	to offer
		and	
			has `ship model: Remnant Satellite`
			not `flagship model: Remnant Satellite`
	on offer
		conversation
			scene "ship/remnant satellite"
			`Upon arriving at Senza Solaria With your Remnant Satellite, before you can even decide where to go, a group of researchers are already there to meet you the moment you step off of your ship.`
			`	"Our scanners detected a ship unknown to them within your fleet, would you be willing to donate it for us to research it?" says a researcher.`
			choice
				`	(Donate the Remnant Satellite to be researched.) WARNING: ALL INSTALLED OUTFITS WILL BE LOST.`
					goto donate
				`	(Don't donate.)`
					defer
			label donate
			`"Ah, perfect! We appreciate your donation, and assure you, your contribution will not go to waste!"`
			`The engineers guide your ship to an isolated landing pad a few miles from the spaceport, and carefully transport it inside of one of their research facilities."`
			``
			`	After idling at the spaceport for a few hours, you hear rumors of a new ship entering production soon at Senza Solaria.`
				accept
	on accept
		take ship `Remnant Satellite`
			"count" 1
		event `Senza Solaria Stocks Remnant Satellite`

		`Kas'lor Ik 582`

mission `Senza Solaria Supply Kas'lor Ik 582`
	invisible
	landing
	source
		planet "Senza Solaria"
	to offer
		and	
			has `ship model: Kas'lor Ik 582`
			not `flagship model: Kas'lor Ik 582`
	on offer
		conversation
			scene "thumbnail/world-ship c"
			`Upon arriving at Senza Solaria With your Kas'lor Ik 582, before you can even decide where to go, a group of researchers are already there to meet you the moment you step off of your ship.`
			`	"Our scanners detected a ship unknown to them within your fleet, would you be willing to donate it for us to research it?" says a researcher.`
			choice
				`	(Donate the Kas'lor Ik 582 to be researched.) WARNING: ALL INSTALLED OUTFITS WILL BE LOST.`
					goto donate
				`	(Don't donate.)`
					defer
			label donate
			`"Ah, perfect! We appreciate your donation, and assure you, your contribution will not go to waste!"`
			`The engineers guide your ship to an isolated landing pad a few miles from the spaceport, and carefully transport it inside of one of their research facilities."`
			``
			`	After idling at the spaceport for a few hours, you hear rumors of a new ship entering production soon at Senza Solaria.`
				accept
	on accept
		take ship `Kas'lor Ik 582`
			"count" 1
		event `Senza Solaria Stocks Kas'lor Ik 582`

				`	(Donate the Heavy Gust to be researched.) WARNING: ALL INSTALLED OUTFITS WILL BE LOST.`
					goto donate
				`	(Don't donate.)`
					defer
			label donate
			`"Ah, perfect! We appreciate your donation, and assure you, your contribution will not go to waste!"`
			`The engineers guide your ship to an isolated landing pad a few miles from the spaceport, and carefully transport it inside of one of their research facilities."`
			``
			`	After idling at the spaceport for a few hours, you hear rumors of a new ship entering production soon at Senza Solaria.`
				accept
	on accept
		take ship `Heavy Gust`
			"count" 1
		event `Senza Solaria Stocks Heavy Gust`
